Please find below a python script to crawl and extract some data.

```python
# Please install required libraries: 
# pip install pandas numpy requests 

import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import pandas as pd

def get_market_cap(symbol):
    try:
        url = f"https://www.moneycontrol.com/marketdata/today-market-cap/{symbol}"
        response = requests.get(url)
        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')
        market_cap = soup.find('div', attrs={'class': 'Mcap'}).text.strip()
        return market_cap
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error occurred: {e}")

def get_financials(org_name):
    try:
        url = f"https://www.moneycontrol.com/stocks/{org_name}/financials"
        response = requests.get(url)
        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')
        financials = soup.find('table', attrs={'class': 'MCTbl'})
        return financials
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error occurred: {e}")

# to do more 
```

# Please install required libraries:

import requests

    try:

        response = requests.get(url)
        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')
        market_cap = soup.find('div', attrs={'class': 'Mcap'}).text.strip()
        return market_cap
